several key components in the API server:\\n\\n1. **Deprecation Warning Injection** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go):\\n   - `IsDeprecated()` function checks if an API object implements the APILifecycleDeprecated interface and compares the deprecation version with the current server version\\n   - `WarningMessage()` function generates human-readable deprecation warnings that include the deprecation version, removal version (if applicable), and replacement API (if available)\\n   - `RemovedRelease()` function extracts the removal version from objects that implement APILifecycleRemoved interface\\n\\n2. **Removal Version Validation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go):\\n   - `RemoveDeletedKinds()` method removes API kinds and versions that have reached their removal date based on APILifecycleRemoved() versions\\n   - `ShouldServeForVersion()` method determines if a resource should be served based on the removal version and current API server version\\n   - Also checks APILifecycleIntroduced() to ensure a version isn't served before it was introduced\\n   - Supports environment variables (KUBE_APISERVER_STRICT_REMOVED_API_HANDLING_IN_ALPHA, KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE) for controlling removal behavior\\n\\n3. **Minimum Supported API Version Checks** objects that implement APILifecycleRemoved interface\\n\\n2. **Removal Version Validation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go):\\n   - `RemoveDeletedKinds()` method removes API kinds and versions that have reached their removal date based on APILifecycleRemoved() versions\\n   - `ShouldServeForVersion()` method determines if a resource should be served based on the removal version and current API server version\\n   - Also checks APILifecycleIntroduced() to ensure a version isn't served before it was introduced\\n   - Supports environment variables (KUBE_APISERVER_STRICT_REMOVED_API_HANDLING_IN_ALPHA, KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE) for controlling removal behavior\\n\\n3. **Minimum Supported API Version Checks** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go):\\n   - `emulatedStorageVersion()` function selects the appropriate storage encoding version based on the minimum compatibility version\\n   - Skips API versions that were introduced after the minimum compatibility version (using APILifecycleIntroduced())\\n   - Used during the storage factory configuration to ensure compatibility with older client versions\\n\\n4. **Warning Handler Integration** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go):\\n   - `AddWarningsHandler()` wraps route handlers to inject deprecation warnings into HTTP responses via the Warning header\\n\\n5. **Metrics Tracking** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go):\\n   - Tracks deprecated API requests through metrics (requested_deprecated_apis gauge)\\n   - Adds audit annotations to flag deprecated API usage\\n   - Instruments route functions with deprecated flag and removal release information\\n\\n6. **API Installation Flow** (pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go):\\n   - During API server startup, `InstallAPIs()` creates a ResourceExpirationEvaluator based on the current Kubernetes version\\n   - Calls `RemoveDeletedKinds()` before installing any API groups to filter out removed APIs\\n   - Only installs API groups and versions that should be served in the current Kubernetes version\\n\\n7. **Route Installation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go):\\n   - For each API resource, checks if it's deprecated using `IsDeprecated()` \\n   - Extracts the removal release using `RemovedRelease()`\\n   - Generates warning messages using `WarningMessage()`\\n   - Wraps all route handlers with `AddWarningsHandler()` to inject warnings into responses\\n   - Passes deprecation and removal information to `InstrumentRouteFunc()` for metrics tracking\\n\\nThe enforcement chain ensures that:\\n- APIs with removal dates in the past are not served at all\\n- APIs currently marked as deprecated generate warnings in all responses\\n- Clients are informed about which versions will be unavailable and what replacements to use\\n- Metrics and audit logs track deprecated API usage for cluster administrators to monitor migration progress\"\n}\n","numLines":108,"startLine":1,"totalLines":108}}}
